I have included here the most important texts I consulted in writing the book (in the case of prolific authors not all their books 
are referenced). Grant and Sloniowski, Warren and Izod, et al. are all essay collections featuring authors I have referred to in 
the text. The place where I and almost everybody else started was, of course, Erik Barnouw.
